Current Affairs Commentary

This Year

Our Country's Education in the Past Year

The weather is cold, and the year is drawing to a close. The rustling fallen leaves tell us that we have reached the end of another year.

Although a year is but a fleeting moment, like a horse glimpsing through a crack, in the endless flow of time, there is still a need for a general summary of the great changes and vicissitudes of the human world in the past year in the annals of human history. Especially for our country, in this year, the flooding of rivers, the coercion of strong neighbors, the cries of hunger and cold, and the contests of heroes of the times, whether tragic, desolate, or farcical, all have value in being reported on as a summary in the long prologue of history.

Here, in the next few days, we will make a general report on the domestic and foreign affairs of our country in the past year. Now, let's start with education.

Because politics in our country is not on track, education has also not been able to progress. Compared with the civilized and advanced countries of Europe and America, there is a vast difference. According to the statistics released by the Ministry of Education this year, in terms of numerical records, there are 34 universities in the country, of which private

Page 6

schools account for nine. There are 18 specialized schools, of which law schools account for five, while industrial schools account for only three, and agricultural schools only two. There are 1,339 secondary schools, with an average of about 300,000 people for each secondary school. The number of secondary school students is 234,811, with an average of about 1,700 people for each secondary school student. There are only 37,604 female secondary school students, accounting for only 16% of the total number of secondary school students. Judging from these figures, the decline of education in our country is undeniable. The education of a country represents a culture. The decline of education in our country is so severe that people lack spiritual food. Illiterates account for more than 80% of the country's population. How can the country not be poor and weak? How can it not be in such a precarious situation today? As for the government's education policy and the trend of thought of students across the country, it is also necessary to make a general review here, because from this, we can glimpse the turning point of history and see the direction of social progress. In 1927, the Northern Expedition of the Party Army aroused the whole country. In particular, young students were practically engaged in the revolutionary movement, and their dedication and sacrifice did leave indelible achievements. With the Party and the country settled, the world won on horseback must not be governed on horseback. Therefore, what the government sought from education at this time was stillness, peace, and the revival of the sacred teachings of loyalty, filial piety, propriety, and righteousness. What was required of students and young people was obedience, studying to save the country, and keeping to their duties. In December of 1930, Chairman Chiang, in his busy schedule, also personally took charge of education, which shows his emphasis on education. In that month, the Executive Yuan sternly ordered the Ministry of Education to rectify the academic atmosphere, saying, "From now on, the government's policy will be to devote all its efforts to improving education. The President of the Executive Yuan, also in charge of administration, should exert his mental and physical abilities to rectify the academic atmosphere. Hereafter, students in all schools must cultivate their character and work hard in their studies. Opposing the principal is no different from opposing the government. They should concentrate on learning and cultivating their minds and bodies, revering the ancient people's precept of not overstepping their bounds, and following the Three Principles of the People of the Premier as their guide." Chairman Chiang also issued a proclamation to students across the country in his capacity as President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Education. The proclamation stated, "Zhongzheng (Chiang's given name) has learned that the country's future is in great crisis, and what causes hidden concerns is the corruption of the academic atmosphere and the rise of student unrest in schools across the country. If this is not immediately and strictly corrected, it will be like a flood that will cause endless harm." It also said, "In the past, military force has swept away the obstacles of revolution. From now on, we should use cultural governance to promote the scale of political tutelage. We vow to improve

education and rectify the academic atmosphere as the most urgent task. I hope that young students across the country will value integrity, uphold practical learning, and be loyal followers of the Three Principles of the People. Do not be misled by heresies, do not stray from the right path, respect teachers, value scholarship, establish oneself and help others, and save oneself and save the country." From the Executive Yuan's order and Chairman Chiang's proclamation, isn't it clear to the whole country that the government requires education to be static and students to bury themselves in their studies?

In July, the Executive Yuan further ordered the Ministry of Education to issue a circular to all directly affiliated agencies and schools to promote morality and make and hang plaques, establishing the eight characters of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, harmony, and peace as the essential principles for educating the people, and to promote China's inherent morality. In the provinces, the Hunan Provincial Government requested the Ministry of Education to improve textbooks. The request stated, "Before 1919, the Chinese textbooks in schools still had literary principles. Recently, the textbooks are often filled with the words 'dog says, pig says, duck says,' as well as 'Miss Cat, Brother Dog, Grandpa Cow.' Animals can speak human words, and respectful titles are added to animals. The language is vulgar and strange beyond description." The authorities in Jilin banned vernacular writing, considering it superficial and empty, and completely useless. They added the teaching of classics and strictly prohibited singing and dancing, considering it the behavior of prostitutes, revealing madness and losing all dignity. Publicly playing and teasing is not pleasing to the eye. These are the reasons why the Jilin education authorities banned singing and dancing. The Shandong Provincial Government suggested reviving the Temple of Confucius. Central Committee members Dai Jitao and Liu Jiwen advocated repairing the Yan Temple, the Zisi Temple, and the tombs of Confucius and Mencius, as well as establishing regulations for sacrificial officials. Zhuang Songfu, deputy director of the Huai River Water Conservancy Commission, proposed two proposals to the National Assembly: implementing the rites and teachings to cultivate the people's virtue and promoting public opinion to understand the people's feelings. During this period, the extreme restoration of education and the extreme reversal of culture were even more obvious facts. This was the peak of the Party government's restoration movement in education.

At the same time, during this period, while the government was vigorously restoring the old in its education policy, it also expressed its determination to establish an education fund and guarantee its independence. In February, the Executive Yuan ordered the Ministry of Finance to earnestly implement the Measures for Guaranteeing the Independence of Education Funds submitted by the Ministry of Education. The provisional constitution passed by the National Assembly also clearly stipulated that "the central and local governments should raise the necessary funds for education as widely as possible, and the funds that are legally independent should be guaranteed." And Hu Hanmin's remarks on rectifying the academic atmosphere clearly opposed the intrusion of bureaucratic politics into the education sector. These were all concrete manifestations of the government's active engagement in rectifying education.

However, this attempt ultimately failed. The continuous student unrest and the wave of teachers and staff striking for salaries finally shattered the government's attempt to rectify education. From last year to this year, the schools that have experienced student unrest include Guangzhou Zhongda, Shanghai Guanghua, Zhonggong Labor University, Nanyang Medical College, Anhui University, Northeast University, Beiping Normal University, Min University, Tsinghua University, Henan University, Henan Provincial No. 1 Middle School, Nanjing Central Military Academy, Jinan Women's Normal School, Shanxi No. 1 Normal School, Xiamen Shuangshi Middle School, as well as Jilin. They were vigorous and echoed each other. On the other hand, because the independence of education funds could not be realized in practice, the wave of strikes for salaries also flourished throughout the country. There were appeals from the education sector in Anhui to repay the accumulated arrears, the eighth representative conference of teachers and staff in Jiangsu Province, all primary and secondary schools in Shanxi Province, and all primary and secondary schools in Beiping. It was a very common phenomenon that teachers and staff in various places and schools were striking for salaries because there was no money for education and teachers and staff could not maintain their lives and were not at ease in their work. In addition, the army often massacred young people, such as the massacre of students in Sichuan. Under these circumstances, how could the government rectify education?

Therefore, the government's attempt to rectify education ultimately failed miserably under the contradictions of subjective conditions and objective environment.

Here, the government has changed direction again. This direction is to promote vocational education and labor education, and to promote scholarship funds and send Party members to study abroad as another policy to stabilize the psychology of young people. The Ministry of Education has clearly ordered the promotion of vocational education and labor education. The National Assembly had the same resolution. The so-called scholarship funds have been established in many schools in various places. This is obviously a measure of last resort. However, unfortunately, it is precisely at this time when people's minds are in turmoil, compounded by domestic disasters and foreign troubles. Young students are internally affected by the desolation of the cries of the disaster victims, and externally affected by the insatiable aggression of strong neighbors. At the same time, they have witnessed the government's calm perfunctoriness and indecisiveness. Therefore, they have spontaneously risen up to save themselves and save the country. They have established volunteer armies, organized anti-Japanese associations, and run around calling for action. From petitions to demonstrations, disturbances and conflicts have occurred in various provinces, such as Nanjing, Shanghai, Shanxi, Guangdong, Hunan, and Hangzhou. The actions are consistent, like fire and tea, and cannot be stopped. Here, it is clearly indicated that students and young people have moved from uneasiness about studying to direct action. At the same time, it is clearly indicated that the government requires the restoration of education, while students have taken the initiative to push it forward. What the government requires is stillness, but in fact, it has become movement, disturbance, and uneasiness. This must have its inevitability and is by no means accidental. Grasping this inevitability and grasping the fundamental meaning of education to determine how to lead young people and educate young people is the current responsibility of educators.

This is the achievement and direction of education in our country in 1931. We hope that 1932 will have better achievements and a more correct direction.

Domestic Important Telegrams Two

Sun Ke Returned to Nanjing Yesterday

Li Zongren, Huang Shaoxiong, and others traveled with him

(Nanjing) Sun Ke, Li Wenfan, Zou Lu, Chen Mingshu, Li Zongren, Li Jishen, Huang Shaoxiong, Chen Ce, Zhang Huichang, Chen Qingyun, Liu Luyin, Deng Qingyang, Zhan Jusi, and others arrived in Nanjing at 10:10 pm on the 27th. Wu Tiecheng, He Yingqin, Zeng Zhongming, and others, as well as the National Government Military Band, were all at the station to welcome them. After arriving in Nanjing, Sun and others went to the official residence of the Ministry of Railways to rest. (Special telegram on the 27th)

(Nanjing) Sun Ke and Li Wenfan went to Shanghai. It is now learned that they will come to Nanjing with Chen Mingshu, Zou Lu, and others by car at 3:00 pm or later on the 27th. (Special telegram on the 27th)

(Nanjing) Li Zongren, Li Jishen, and others entered Nanjing from Shanghai with Sun Ke and others on the 27th. The reception office has prepared accommodation at the Central Hotel. (Special telegram on the 27th)

(Nanjing) Wang Faqin has a cold and has not gone out or seen guests. (Special telegram on the 27th)

Hu Hanmin's Reply to Lin Sen's Telegram

Blood Pressure Still High, Unable to Travel North

(Nanjing) Hu Hanmin replied to Lin Sen on the 26th, saying, "Upon receiving your telegram, I am earnestly instructed to come to Nanjing, which is too much of a demand and makes me both grateful and sad. The general situation of my illness has been reported to you in the telegrams from Xiaoma. I have been through decades of revolution and have suffered many hardships. Now that the country is in urgent danger and a new opportunity has just begun, how dare I be idle? However, since the spring of this year, I have suddenly suffered an unexpected change. I have been living in seclusion for eight months, and my mental and physical strength have been greatly damaged. Earlier, when the rebellion occurred in Shandong Province, those in charge were almost dumbfounded and helpless and did nothing. I deeply regretted that the country would be destroyed soon and the foundation of the Party would be overturned. At the request of all parties, I went to Shanghai to promote peace despite my illness. Then, following the doctor's advice, I transferred to Hong Kong for recuperation. However, there were disputes at the Fourth Plenary Session in Guangdong, and I again stood up to mediate despite my long illness. For the past two months, I have been exhausted, but unscrupulous people are still fabricating rumors and slandering me everywhere. You must know this news, and I need not elaborate. The reform of the Party and government is the most urgent task today. I have always held this view, and I have already shed tears for my comrades in Beijing. Recently, I also telegraphed Jingwei, Zhesheng, and Tiyun to discuss together. We should say everything we know and say everything to the best of our ability. I believe that the people's hearts are the Party's base. Today's affairs are not just about fighting for a day's length, nor are they about the actions of one hand or one foot. We should seek spiritual unity, and the form should not be restricted. If we can meet each other with sincerity, then our intentions should be consistent. My blood pressure is still high. Today's examination still shows 115 degrees. The doctor said that if I do not rest, I will have a stroke at any time. Therefore, I am uneasy and unable to travel north. I am saddened and hurried to reply, hoping for your understanding." (Special telegram on the 27th)

Feng Yuxiang's Special Train Passed Through Jinan Yesterday Afternoon

Feng Talked About the Significance of Going to Beijing in Three Ways

Published a Letter to Compatriots on the Way

(Tianjin) Feng Yuxiang's special train passed through Fengtai at 10:00 am on the 27th, Luofa at 11:00 am, and arrived in Tianjin at 12:40 pm. Wang Yimin, the director of the Public Security Bureau, led a security team and a military band to the main station to guard the area. Sun Chuanfang, Cheng Ke, Lin Shuyan, Lu Chengwu, Dong Xicheng, and more than 10 others arrived at the station to welcome him. Wang Shuchang and Zhou Longguang, the provincial and municipal authorities, did not arrive at the station. Wang sent Chief of Staff Liu Jialuan to represent him in welcoming him. Those who traveled with Feng included Central Committee member Liu Shouzhong, aides Gao Xingya, Li Xingzhong, Wang Shijiu, He Chuqiang, Lei Jishang, Guo Zengkai, Zhang Shengsan, Wang Daoyu, Ding Shuben, and more than a dozen members of the pistol team. Feng wore a blue cloth cotton-padded jacket and a gray cloth cloak, looking like a countryman. Feng got off the train, shook hands with those who welcomed him, and repeatedly said that he was sorry to have troubled everyone to come and greet him in such cold weather. He then agreed to be photographed by reporters from various newspapers and went into the car with Sun Chuanfang and others to talk. The car then turned to the Jinpu Road and headed south. The reporters also boarded the car to the West Station and had a ten-minute conversation with Feng. Feng said, "When I arrive in Nanjing, I will focus on foreign affairs. Seeing that Japan has trampled on the three northeastern provinces, we cannot but think of a way. Therefore, I have many proposals that I want to put forward at the First Plenary Session of the Central Committee. Now that there are no obstacles in politics, everyone will be able to unite and find a way for diplomacy and put politics on track. Furthermore, Nanjing is surrounded by the guns of imperialism and is not suitable as a capital. I intend to move it to the interior of China to ensure safety." At this point, the car arrived at the West Station. The reporters and Sun Chuanfang and others got off the train. Han Fuju and Shi Yousan sent telegrams and sent representatives to Dezhou to welcome him. (Special telegram on the 26th)

(Beiping) Feng Yuxiang passed through Fengtai at 8:30 am this morning and went to Tianjin. Feng wore a blue cloth jacket and trousers and rode in a closed railway car and a freight car. Aides Liu Shouzhong, Yun Rong, Lei Jishang, and a hundred members of the guard training regiment accompanied him. Zhang Xueliang sent Bao Wenxue to Fengtai to welcome him. Feng said that he had received successive telegrams from the central government summoning him to attend the First Plenary Session of the Central Committee. He said that he did not dare to accept the welcome along the way. "The plan to save the country cannot be exhausted in one word. The whole country should unite and differences of opinion should be resolved through political means, not through war. The Party should be close to the people, and politics should be open and honest. A unified government should be formed, and preparations should be made for war against Japan and the recovery of lost territory." Yan Xishan could not come because his father was still ill. He highly praised Wang Jingwei's meeting to save the country. He said that there were three points to going to Beijing this time: (1) The Japanese army's attack on Jinzhou was very urgent; (2) To promote national unity; (3) To quickly recover the lost territory. Feng reported his itinerary to Wang Jingwei and Hu Hanmin in a telegram from Shijiazhuang. He also published a letter to his compatriots on the way, saying that in order to jointly meet the national crisis, he resolutely came to Beijing to attend the First Plenary Session of the Central Committee. He will put forward the following specific opinions: 1. Representatives from various mass organizations should quickly organize a National Salvation Conference to supervise all major diplomatic, domestic, and military plans during the national crisis. 2. Establish a National Defense Committee to unify military organizations and military command, select strong troops, and move them to the forefront and other important areas to implement the recovery of lost territory by force. 3. Give pensions to the martyrs who died in previous revolutionary battles and the current anti-Japanese war to encourage morale. Feng believes that the above three items are the current urgent tasks to save the country. He has telegraphed a detailed plan to the First Plenary Session of the Central Committee and requested a public decision. He called on all compatriots and all comrades of the Party to work together to promote its realization, upholding the spirit of peace, struggle, and saving China of Mr. Sun Yat-sen. (Special telegram on the 27th)

(Beiping) Feng Yuxiang's entourage said that Feng had previously lived outside Fenyang City, Shanxi Province, with Li Dequan, first in Yudao River, and then bought a mill near Shidun'an, 30 miles from the city. He lived there and ate noodles, and he personally milled the flour. Every morning, he went around the mountains for a week and returned to read and practice calligraphy. He read social science books. Feng established a civilian primary school nearby, providing students with food and drink. There were more than 100 students. (Special telegram on the 27th)

(Taiyuan) Feng Yuxiang submitted a total of three proposals to the Central Plenary Session. The full text has been telegraphed to Beijing. The main text and measures of each proposal are as follows: (A) Proposal for Mass Supervision of the Government: In order to prepare for the war against Japan in the face of the national crisis, mass organizations should supervise the government and military organs, as well as the troops in various places. 1. A National Salvation Conference should be established as soon as possible. Branches of the National Salvation Conference should be established in various provinces, cities, and counties, organized by representatives of purely mass organizations. The members are as follows: (1) Farmers' organizations; (2) Workers' organizations; (3) Businessmen's organizations; (4) Journalists; (5) Educators; (6) Important production organizations; (7) Other occupational combinations; (8) Party departments at all levels. The tasks of the National Salvation Conference are: (1) Supervising government administration; (2) Auditing government revenue and expenditure; (3) Matters that should be promoted or abolished should be discussed and handed over to the government for implementation; (4) If the National Salvation Conference considers an official to be corrupt or derelict in his duties, it may petition his directly superior organ to suspend the war and hand him over to judicial judgment. The National Salvation Conference at all levels has the power to supervise the troops fighting against foreign countries at the front and may control their retreat in the face of battle. It may also supervise and audit the military discipline and military supplies of the local garrison troops. (B) Proposal for Recovering Lost Territory by Force: (1) Main text: Implement the recovery of the lost territory in Northeast China by force. (2) Measures: Organize a National Defense Committee, unify steelmaking, steel production, and arsenals, and build the interior. (3) Select strong troops and concentrate them at the forefront and other important areas. (4) Implement conscription. (5) Implement national mobilization. (C) Proposal for Giving Pensions to Deceased Officers and Soldiers: (1) Main text: In order to prepare for war against foreign countries, pensions and awards should be given to the officers and soldiers who died in previous revolutionary battles and the anti-Japanese war to strengthen the faith of officers and soldiers. (2) Measures: (1) Worship the deceased officers and soldiers. (2) Give pensions to the families of the deceased officers and soldiers. (3) Welfare homes and factories should be established to accommodate the disabled officers and soldiers. Those who are injured and meritorious should be given separate awards to encourage them. (4) Establish schools for the children of military officers and soldiers. (5) Establish a special management agency and designate special funds. (26th)

(Jinan) Feng Yuxiang's special train passed through Dezhou at 9:35 pm and came south. It is expected to pass through Jinan at 12:00. Preparations are being made here to welcome him. The station is heavily guarded. (Special telegram on the 27th)

(Nanjing) Central Committee member Feng Yuxiang and Liu Shouzhong went south to attend the plenary session. Two Suggestions for Military System

(Nanjing) Swiss General Sonderer has made some suggestions on China's military system, saying that China's military expenditure reaches as much as 434 million yuan per year, but it does not actually help national defense. This is the malpractice of mercenary soldiers. We should quickly switch to conscription and militia systems so that military expenditure can be reduced and the number of combatants can be increased. If we switch to conscription, with one-year discharges, it will only account for 40% of the current military expenditure, and we can obtain 6 million combatants in ten years. If we train militias, the number will be even greater. Because the four countries of Germany, Austria, Hungary, and Bohemia were punished by the Paris Peace Conference, they were restricted from using conscription. Why should China impose restrictions on itself and not adopt the conscription system? Furthermore, Wu Guang, our military attaché in Germany, suggested that conscription and militia should be used together. The number of militiamen who enlist in our country every year is over 500,000, and it is not difficult to draw one in a thousand. Conscription should be limited to 300,000 regular troops, with one batch of infantry discharged every year and cavalry, artillery, and special forces every two years. We only need to spend the military salary of 300,000 men each year, and after ten years, the call-up of militiamen and conscripts can reach 5 million people. Therefore, the reason why the militia is the main force is to save money and stabilize production. If the militia is formed on the spot, it can easily deal with any banditry in the area. Because the people of our country think that tribes are more important than the country, it is enough to give the militia the responsibility of self-defense to give play to their natural tendencies. (Special telegram on the 27th)

Foreign Important Telegrams

Lancashire Cotton Industry Brewing Strike

National News Agency, Manchester, 26th: The Lancashire cotton industry is on the verge of a strike in the new year. 500,000 workers will be affected. The main reason is the increase in working hours, followed by the reduction of wages and the reduction of staff. In the past two years, the cotton industry has often been in a state of decline and unrest, either due to strikes by workers or shutdowns by factory owners. Recently, the Cotton Spinners' and Manufacturers' Association announced that it would terminate the 1919 working hours and wage contract on December 31. The contract stipulates a 48-hour work week and a 30% increase in wages. Later, wages were reduced by 12.5%. It is now heard that the Association wants to restore the 52.5-hour work week and reduce wages by another 12.5%. If the Manufacturers' Association also joins the Cotton Spinners' and Manufacturers' Association, 200,000 people will be directly affected, and another 300,000 people are likely to be affected as well. However, the Manufacturers' Association itself is also in dispute with workers over increasing the number of looms managed per worker, and no solution has been reached. The Association has now decided to ask its branches to express their views on the decision of the Cotton Spinners' and Manufacturers' Association. The factory workers in Lancashire are now very angry and have organized an office to actively promote their cause. Union leaders have also stated that they intend to persevere to the end. If the factory owners do not make concessions, a strike on January 1st is likely unavoidable. The factory workers are particularly angry about the restoration of the 52.5-hour work week, saying that if this is the case, they will have to get up earlier and start work at 6:00 a.m.

All India Congress Chairman Nehru Prepares to Welcome Gandhi, Arrested

Situation Unstable on the Northwest Frontier of India

Havas, Allahabad, 26th: Yesterday morning, Nehru, Chairman of the Indian National Congress, was about to set off to prepare for welcoming Gandhi, who will arrive in Bombay on Sunday, when he was suddenly arrested by the police. Upon hearing the news, the Congress Committee cancelled all the welcoming ceremonies for Gandhi and announced a "day of mourning" to protest. Many members of the Volunteer Corps immediately took cars to various places to spread the news of Nehru's arrest and distribute declarations issued by the Committee, calling on workers everywhere to stop work. Telegrams from all over India stated that the Congress Committee was encouraging the people not to pay rent, and the non-resistance movement seemed to be reactivated. The situation on the Northwest Frontier of India has also become unstable again. Communist leader Abdu Ghaffar Khan and many of his followers were arrested for advocating independence in violation of orders and have been exiled to Bengal. Eighteen representatives of the Round Table Conference returned to Bombay yesterday and issued a declaration stating that the Round Table Conference has not failed. Whether the results achieved can be effective depends entirely on the Indians themselves.

Havas, Peshawar, 26th: The situation in the Northwest Frontier Provinces of India is currently extremely unstable. Therefore, the police stations arrested many members of illegal organizations and Communist agitators yesterday and today.

Plot to Assassinate Japanese Ambassador to Russia Hirota Case

Czech Government Suspects Russian Intelligence Deliberately Fabricated

National News Agency, Prague, 26th: The Czech government authorities do not believe the rumor that Werner, an official of the Czech diplomatic office in Russia, plotted to assassinate Hirota, the Japanese ambassador to Russia. It is said that Werner had a disagreement with the Russian intelligence authorities and was therefore framed. Werner is gentle in nature and has never been fond of risky undertakings. He has also served as the secretary of the Russian office for five years. Before this incident, the Czech authorities had planned to promote him.

National News Agency, Moscow, 26th: The conspiracy of a Soviet citizen to assassinate Japanese Ambassador Hirota is still attracting attention here. According to various indications, this matter may not be ended merely by recalling a certain diplomatic official who was the mastermind. There may be important repercussions.

Japanese Parliament Elects Standing Committee Members

Cabinet Approves Previous Government Budget

Kwantung Governor Tsukamoto Submits Resignation

Nippon Rengo, Tokyo, 27th: The House of Peers held a formal meeting at 9:00 a.m. this morning. After unanimously passing the House of Peers' response to the Emperor, the chairman of the entire House was elected. As a result, Yoritoshi Matsudaira was elected. The meeting resumed at 10:45 a.m. Speaker Tokugawa read the Imperial Rescript and issued various reports. He also reported the names of the elected standing committee members. The resolution to extend condolences to the Manchurian Expeditionary Force was then passed. Finally, Speaker Tokugawa stated, "If no unexpected events occur, this House intends to adjourn until January 21, Showa 7." There were no objections and the meeting adjourned at 11:15 a.m.

Today's House of Representatives meeting was convened at 10:39 a.m. The resolution to extend condolences to the Manchurian Expeditionary Force was passed, and the standing committee members below the chairman of the entire House were elected. Yoshisawa of the Minseito Party was elected as the chairman of the entire House. The session was adjourned at 11:25 a.m. and reconvened at 12:05 p.m. to report the results of the election and resolve to hold plenary meetings on Tuesdays, Thursdays, and Saturdays (committee meetings on Mondays, Wednesdays, and Fridays, Tuesdays for questions). The meeting adjourned at 12:13 p.m. The results of the mutual election of the chairmen of the standing committees of the House of Representatives were all dominated by the opposition parties. Kawasaki was the chairman of the Budget Committee, Okazaki was the chairman of the Settlement Committee, Nagata was the chairman of the Petition Committee, and Fujita was the chairman of the Punishment Committee.

Nippon Rengo, Tokyo, 27th: Kwantung Governor Tsukamoto

scheduled to meet with Prime Minister Wakatsuki today to formally submit his resignation. Wakatsuki met with the Prime Minister yesterday and today to discuss the selection of candidates. Currently, Manosuke Yamaoka is the most highly regarded.

Reuters, Tokyo, 27th: The current government does not have time to calmly rewrite the entire budget for next year, so it has to accept the budget prepared by the previous government as a basis for calculation. However, the final budget figures have been significantly changed compared to those proposed by the previous government. It was approved by the cabinet today. Expenditures have been reduced by approximately 100 million yen. The total amount of expenditures approved by the cabinet today is 1,397 million yen. The amount proposed by former Finance Minister Inoue was 1,480 million yen. The most significant reduction this time is the unemployment relief project, and the debt reduction reserve fund has also been reduced by 30 million yen. The administrative expenses for Sakhalin Island have also been reduced by 15 million yen. The policy of not borrowing money has now been abandoned. In order to offset revenue and expenditure, it will raise 191 million yen in debt. The new budget stipulates naval expenditures of 211 million yen and army expenditures of 183 million yen.

Important News

Capital Citizens Support the Grand Meeting for Peaceful Reunification

Various agencies, groups, and people from all walks of life in the capital held a grand meeting at the public sports field at 10:00 a.m. on the 27th to support peaceful reunification and urge the Central Committee members to jointly alleviate the national crisis. Zhou Bomin, representing the municipal party department, Ni Guanghe, representing the agricultural sector, Jing Songquan, representing the industrial sector, Mu Huaxuan, representing the business sector, and Luo Ciqi, representing the overseas Chinese, served as the presidium of the meeting. On the Central Committee side, Li Liejun, Jing Hengyi, and Shang Zhen attended. Approximately 5,000 representatives from various agencies and people's organizations attended. Chairman Zhou Bomin presided over the ceremony. After the ceremony, the chairman reported the significance of the meeting, stating that since the Party lost its cohesive force, internal political disturbances have lost their center of operation, and external powers are coveting and taking the opportunity to occupy our territory. The national situation is in danger, and people are panicked. Fortunately, the advanced members of the Party feel that in this critical situation, there is no solution except to unite and strive for peaceful reunification. Now, all parties are working together, and peaceful reunification has been successfully achieved. The significance of today's meeting is (1) to hope that the Party will improve Party affairs and political organization with a spirit of great unity and permanently lay the foundation for peaceful reunification. In the future, anyone who undermines peaceful reunification will be the public enemy of the people. (2) To hope that the unified government will relieve all the suffering of the people after its establishment so that the people can obtain genuine benefits. (3) To hope that all the people will have the determination to sacrifice and fight, concentrate their strength, and serve as the government's backing to jointly overthrow Japanese imperialism. Next, Central Committee member Jing Hengyi gave a speech, stating that Japan is showing its violence, abandoning all international treaties and credibility, and the world's justice, and is not satisfied with occupying our Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang provinces, but is launching a large-scale attack on our Jinzhou. This barbaric act is indeed intolerable by justice. However, if our people only know how to rely on justice and do not immediately mobilize to resist violence, they are actually abdicating their duty. However, our national education is too incomplete, and even compared with Japan, it is inevitably inferior. This is a fundamental and major problem. As a member of the education community, I speak of education in terms of education, so I sincerely hope that national education will become more and more developed to enrich the strength of the people. Next, Li Liejun gave a speech, stating that today's national affairs are urgent. In terms of external aggression, it is even worse than the Sino-British War, the Sino-French War, the Sino-Japanese War of Jiawu, and the Boxer Rebellion. In terms of the domestic disturbances in the past few years, it is even worse than the Spring and Autumn Period, the Warring States Period, the Six Dynasties, and the Five Dynasties. This is truly a critical moment for the nation's survival. It is time for our comrades and compatriots to die for the country. We are instructed to peacefully reunify and jointly face the national crisis. We came to Beijing for this purpose. Since we have been entrusted with the task, we must work harder. However, in order to jointly face the national crisis, we must unite the strength of the entire people and be of one mind and one heart. However, empty words are of no use. If we really want to achieve the goal of saving the country, we must quickly publicize the power to the people so that the people can directly and indirectly participate in politics and embark on the road of people's politics so that the power of the people throughout the country can be used. Li Liejun has proposed to his comrades in Beijing to implement civil rights, carry out constitutionalism, and elect county magistrates, but these proposals have not been adopted, which is very regrettable. However, at this serious moment, the people at the conference are working hard to find a way to save the situation, and the people must still unite and work hard and not abandon their responsibility and work together to solve it. Next, Shang Zhen gave a speech, painfully stating the urgency of the situation in Jinzhou. If Jinzhou is not defended, then all parts of North China will be shaken. Therefore, the government and the people must cooperate to resist aggression, otherwise, the danger of national destruction will be imminent. Now, the Party's unity and political unification should have a true spirit and be carried through to the end, not just in form. Next, overseas Chinese representative Luo Ciqi and others gave speeches in succession, and then the following proposals were passed: (1) Send a telegram to the whole country to support peaceful reunification and vow to use the power of the people to permanently stop any civil war. (2) Send a telegram to all members of the Central Committee, asking them to follow their conscience, unite sincerely, and jointly face the national crisis. (3) Send a telegram to leaders such as Wang Jingwei, Hu Hanmin, and Chiang Kai-shek, asking them to come to Beijing immediately to jointly govern the central government. (4) Request the Central Government to telegraph Zhang Xueliang to defend Jinzhou with all his strength. (5) Request the Central Government to quickly send elite troops to recover the lost territories. (6) Request the Central Government to request the United States to immediately convene the signatory countries of the Washington Nine-Power Treaty to sanction the violent Japan. (7) Request the Central Government to determine its diplomatic policy and vigorously implement revolutionary diplomacy. (8) Request the Central Government to concentrate diplomatic talents and quickly strengthen the embassies and consulates. (9) Request the Central Government to formulate a national defense plan. (10) Request the Central Government to implement a conscription system. (11) Request the Central Government to rectify discipline and purify internal affairs. (12) Request the Central Government to convene a national salvation conference as soon as possible. (13) Effectively guarantee the people's various freedoms. (14) Request the Central Government to support the people's movement and restore its vertical organization. (15) Request the Central Government to strictly prohibit the military from interfering in politics. (16) Oppose the establishment of political subcommittees and military region systems to avoid the development of separatist situations. Finally, the meeting ended with slogans.

Feng and Yan Decide to Go to Beijing

They Have Already Discussed Everything in Lancun

And Sent Telegrams to Wang and Hu to Solicit Opinions

Taiyuan Correspondence: Yan and Feng, who have been separated for over a year, have achieved unity due to the current national crisis. The First Plenary Session of the Central Committee has already opened in Beijing, and Lin Sen and others have sent telegrams urging them to go to Beijing to attend, believing that it is necessary to meet and discuss. Therefore, they mutually agreed and invited Zhao Daiwen and Liu Shouchong, two Central Committee members in Taiyuan, to meet yesterday (the 23rd) at Jinshan Middle School in Lancun, because the area is relatively quiet and can avoid the hustle and bustle. The situation in Taiyuan and Lancun yesterday is recorded separately below:

Feng Passes Through Taiyuan: Feng was originally scheduled to depart from Fenyang at 7:00 AM to go to Taiyuan and then to Lancun. However, due to a farewell meeting held by students from various schools in Fenyang before his departure, he was slightly delayed and did not depart until 8:30 AM. His accompanying staff included Li Xingzhong, Wang Sijiu, He Chuqiang, Ying Yiquan, Lei Jishang, and Guo Zengkai, a total of six people, traveling in two cars. They stopped to refuel in Wenshui, and Feng walked seven or eight li, so he did not arrive in Taiyuan until after 11:00 AM. Military and political figures such as Yang Aiyuan, Sun Chu, Li Fuying, Wang Jingguo, Rong Honglu, Zhou Dai, Wang Ping, Wang Xifu, Li Shangren, Shao Xiuwen, and Chen Zengzhi all went to meet him at the New South Gate Bus Station. After Feng got out of the car, he shook hands with each of the welcomers, repeatedly saying, "In this cold weather, I am really sorry to trouble you all." His staff distributed short declarations (see below). Feng wore a short blue cotton jacket, with a blue cotton padded coat and trousers underneath, and blue cloth single-strap cotton shoes, blue cloth socks, and a snuff-colored felt hat, completely dressed as a countryman. He nodded frequently, his smile amiable, and his spirits were excellent. By this time, the platform was crowded with welcoming students and representatives of various groups, who applauded when they saw Feng arrive. The crowds watching on both sides also applauded. After walking a few steps, he was accompanied by Yang Aiyuan and others to get into a car to rest at the second guesthouse of the Provincial Government on Xinmin Street. He exchanged greetings with the officials for about ten minutes. Most of the welcomers then excused themselves, and Feng personally saw them to the gate before returning. After a short rest, he took a car to visit Central Committee member Liu Shouchong at No. 7 Xinmin West Street. After talking for half an hour, he and Liu took a car out of the Small North Gate and drove to Lancun. Yang Aiyuan, Wang Ping, and others also went by car one after another.

Yan Arrives at Lancun: Yan set off from Hebian at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. His entourage included Du Chunyi, Li Guanyang, Ning Chaowu, and Wang Zunguang, traveling in two cars. They arrived at Jinshan Middle School in Lancun at 11:00 AM and immediately went to the teaching office to rest and wait for Feng. Yan's spirit was better than last year's. He wore a small melon-shaped hat, a blue satin mandarin jacket, a gray cloth cotton robe, and gray cloth cotton trousers, with grayish-white woolen socks on his feet. Zhao Daiwen arrived at Lancun at 10:00 AM. Yan had a long talk with Zhao and met with Li Fuying, Wang Xifu, and others who had arrived before Feng. For a while, Yan went out of the school to tour the mountains and watch the springs. After half an hour, Feng and Liu Shouchong arrived, and Zhao Daiwen went out to greet them, shook hands, and bid farewell, then led them to the small rest area in the inner courtyard.

Yan and Feng Meet: Soon Yan returned, walking to the inner courtyard, repeatedly saying, "Mr. Feng has arrived, Mr. Feng has arrived!" When he entered the room, he rushed forward to shake hands with Feng in greeting, each saying "Long time no see, long time no see," and smiled at each other. Then, he dismissed the others, and only Yan, Feng, Liu, Zhao, and Yang Aiyuan remained in the room. They immediately had a very thorough discussion on their future positions on the current situation and the proposals for the First Plenary Session of the Central Committee. They dispersed at 3:00 PM. Then, Ning Chaowu and Gao Xingya drafted a telegram. Yan, Feng, Liu, and Zhao went to the courtyard to take a group photo. Yan and Liu Shouchong, Feng and Zhao Daiwen yielded their positions to each other for a long time. Finally, Yan stood on the right, and his left was in the order of Liu, Zhao, and Feng. After the photo was taken, Feng went to the back mountain with his staff to watch the springs, saying, "Let me open my eyes." He returned after half an hour.

Yan and Feng Give Speeches: Feng then acceded to the request of all the students of Jinshan Middle School and gave a speech in the auditorium. In essence, he expressed extreme dissatisfaction with the authorities' lack of resistance to the recent occupation of the three northeastern provinces by the violent Japanese, and advocated striving for mass movements. Young people should fight and shed blood for this civil right. The only glimmer of hope for China now is that patriotic young people can rise up together to save the country. He hoped that everyone would rush forward. After the speech, there was thunderous applause. Yan also took the stage to speak, saying that China used to seek survival on the basis of equilibrium, but now it can no longer do so. Our country's weakness did not begin today, and it is necessary to prepare for at least twenty years. We should not lightly declare war today, but we must also resist.

Feng's Remarks: After Feng's speech, reporters from various Taiyuan newspapers went forward to request an audience. Feng led them to the conference room and made the following simple remarks: "My political views for the future have been detailed in my reply to Mr. Wang's telegram and the simple declaration I issued today, so I will not repeat them. In short, I advocate active war preparation against Japan and internal unity and cooperation. I will not return to Fenyang and have decided to go to Beijing to attend the Central Committee Plenary Session. Mr. Yan and the two members Liu and Zhao have also decided to go and have telegraphed Mr. Wang and Mr. Hu to solicit their opinions. Once their reply arrives, a decision can be made. I have already telegraphed Mr. Lin Zichao with this intention. I believe that there is nothing that cannot be said to others and I am very willing to meet with you all. I hope to have a long talk with you tomorrow and hope that you will raise more questions so that I can do my best."

Yan's Remarks: The reporters then visited Yan and had a brief question-and-answer session with him: (Question) Mr., what was the result of today's meeting with the members Feng, Liu, and Zhao? (Answer) Faced with the national crisis, it is our inescapable duty. I have decided to do my best and work hard with all the comrades of the party and the country to jointly save the crisis. (Question) What are your views on the current situation? (Answer) The country is so weak that it is already at its limit. We should establish common goals for national salvation, determine a plan of action, catch up quickly, and work together to seek salvation. (Question) Will you and the members Feng, Liu, and Zhao go to Beijing immediately? Has the departure date been determined? (Answer) We have telegraphed Mr. Wang and Mr. Hu, asking them to go to Beijing together. (Question) Can the original text of the telegram that the members sent to Mr. Lin today be published? (Answer) It can be published. The original telegram is as follows: "We have telegraphed comrades Wang and Hu to discuss the departure date. We will reply as soon as we come to Beijing together. (Signed) Yan Xishan, Feng Yuxiang, Liu Shouchong, Zhao Daiwen." (Question) How will the Shanxi massacre be handled? (Answer) I have discussed this matter with Mr. Feng, Liu, and Zhao. We all advocate going together to offer condolences to the injured and dead students, and jointly send a telegram to the Central Committee Plenary Session to report the truth of the incident and request that it be dealt with according to law. (Question) Will you still return to Hebian? (Answer) I will return to Hebian temporarily. (Question) What proposals do you have for the Central Committee Plenary Session? (Answer) I plan to propose two cases: national salvation and self-strengthening. I am currently drafting them. (Note: One is a ten-year self-strengthening plan, which includes military, political, educational, economic, and production development, and the other is a plan for ten thousand elite troops to defend Jinzhou to the death.)

Yan and Feng Return Separately: At about 5:00 PM, Yan, Feng, and the officials went to the dining room for dinner. At 6:00 PM, Feng bid farewell to Yan and returned to the city by car, staying at the office at No. 30 Cangmenqian. At 6:10 PM, Zhao Daiwen and Liu Shouchong also entered the city by car. Yan stayed in Lancun alone, personally organizing the telegrams and proposals. At 7:30 PM, he returned to Hebian by the original car.

Feng's Declaration: Feng issued a simple declaration when he arrived in Taiyuan yesterday, saying, "Fellow compatriots, comrades, Yuxiang has come to Taiyuan this time to work with comrades to overcome the national crisis. The specific views have been detailed in the previous telegram to Mr. Wang Jingwei. I firmly believe that in the future, if China wants to overthrow imperialism externally and eliminate feudal warlords internally, it must support democratic forces and establish democratic politics so that the general revolutionary masses can carry out legitimate struggles with concrete organizations. If the government leaves the masses, it will become counter-revolutionary. If the government does not have a broad mass base, it will soon collapse. Now that autocratic politics has fallen, we must work harder from now on to ensure that the roots of autocratic politics are eradicated in China in the future. The future of the Republic of China will be promising. I, Xiang, uphold this belief and will never waver. I am willing to work with my compatriots throughout the country and comrades in the party to achieve this." Feng Yuxiang, December 23, 1931.

Changes in Zhang Zhankui's Troops in Fengxian County

Party and Government Agencies are Controlled

And Trenches are Being Dug Outside the City

Xuzhou Correspondence: The Third Cavalry Division of Zhang Zhankui has been stationed in Feng, Pei, and Dang counties in northwestern Xuzhou for several months. Zhang's troops are organized according to a three-regiment system, with a total of about 2,000 people. The division headquarters and the first regiment are stationed in Fengxian County, the second regiment is stationed in Zhouzhai, Dangshan County, and the first regiment is stationed in Loulou, Peixian County. However, the pay is insufficient, and most of it is levied locally. Two weeks ago, Zhang borrowed 5,000 yuan from all sectors of Fengxian County to maintain military pay. The county government was responsible for 3,000 yuan, and the chamber of commerce was responsible for 2,000 yuan. Fengcheng is a small area, and its strength is already difficult to overcome. Zhang then borrowed daily maintenance fees from the local area, about 500 yuan, from the county magistrate Yang Liang to convene a meeting of various agency personnel, and decided that it was difficult to comply. Zhang was very dissatisfied and immediately expressed that if there was no money, it would be difficult to maintain military discipline. However, all sectors felt that the money was really not available, and it was difficult to take care of it. At that time, the situation was already serious. Unexpectedly, at 4:00 PM on the 25th, the troops of Zhang's troops stationed in the city suddenly acted freely.

For a while, gunshots rang out everywhere, and important agencies in the city, such as the county government, the party headquarters, the finance department, the agricultural and industrial bank, and the chamber of commerce, were successively controlled, and the county magistrate Yang Liang, the party committee Dong Yuqiu, and other important leaders were all taken into custody. All the police and police guns were confiscated, the city gates were closed to prohibit entry and exit, and the order in the city was in chaos. Fortunately, the merchants and people were not disturbed. The deputy captain of the county police team, Zhang Yaxuan, and the seventh district chief, Wang Chunjiu, disguised themselves and escaped from the city overnight, running to Xuzhou this afternoon (the 26th). They immediately reported to the garrison headquarters. According to Zhang and Wang, when Yu and others left Feng, Zhang's troops outside the city were digging trenches around the city. Before the change, Zhang's troops stationed in Loulou and Zhouzhai had transferred some of their troops to Fengxian County, and the family members of Zhang's division commander had also been sent away from Feng. After the police team surrendered their guns, the officials were forbidden to go out. A platoon leader was injured in the shoulder by Zhang's soldiers because he and Yu and others escaped together, and his military uniform had not been removed. When Yu and others left the city, there was no looting in the city. It is not known what happened at night. The most strange thing is that Zhang's division commander walked along the city, and his troops had acted freely, which is very strange. Yu Qing used a long-distance call to inquire to Fengcheng. Although the line was not broken, he repeatedly shouted without responding. According to legend, the order in Fengcheng was very chaotic. The garrison department paid great attention to this and heard that it would be reported to the authorities for handling. (26th)

Yangzhou

Jiangbei Disaster Victims Obstruct the Operation of Cars: The Zhenyang Road has been unable to travel for more than four months since the autumn floods, resulting in considerable losses for the company. After the water receded, the roads that were submerged were fundamentally redone, and most of the roads that were not submerged were occupied by disaster victims living in sheds nearby. Then, they invested money to obtain relocation. Currently, the car has not been opened for a month, and in the afternoon of the previous day (25), when the car arrived at Hongqiao Town, it was blocked by the disaster victims who had previously lived on the road, claiming that when they moved, they had asked the company staff to help them ask the Justice and Relief Agency for relief, so now they are here to get flour or they will not allow the car to be opened. After the company sent people to explain in detail, and the passengers spoke from the middle again, the car was allowed to go. Unexpectedly, at 9:00 AM yesterday (26), three or four hundred male and female disaster victims gathered again to block the car at the original location yesterday. After the company staff Ma Zhongwen and Hu Ansheng and the Hongqiao Land Station Chief repeatedly persuaded the men to disperse, but the women still refused to retreat. After the morning, local people directly submitted a document to the Justice and Relief Agency to ask for relief, and the company agreed to help from the side. The disaster victims then dispersed.

All Middle Schools Continue to Strike: The middle schools in this county were supposed to resume classes on the 26th. The private Huaizhong Middle School has notified the parents of each student to order the students to go to school. However, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of Students in the county convened a meeting of representatives that night after receiving the letter from the Joint Association of Teachers and Staff of Middle Schools in Jiangsu Province to advise on resuming classes, and decided to continue the strike. The Provincial Middle School even has a declaration of unlimited strike, roughly saying that they will wait until the government sends troops before resuming classes.

Auditing Office Escapes and Arrests Soldiers: On the 24th, Liang's Auditing Office on the 25th Road, Baweigang, Jingjiang, the squad leader Li Shutang and others quarreled with the platoon leader over the sewing of clothes, and angrily took their guns to the south. They lingered in Shengang. The Huang District Chief reported to the county and sent a police team to the countryside to disarm the soldiers and take them to the county on the evening of the 25th. At this time, Hu Hedo, the director of the Baweigang Auditing Office, had learned that the soldiers were being escorted to the county in Chengjie, and immediately sent the auditors Chen Haiying and Liang Fengming and others to cross the river to the south. Hangzhou

A Fire at the New Market Kills Three People: Liu Fengshan's family, No. 9, Dongpo Lane, Dongpo Road, New Market, Hangzhou City, Tianjin, Liu Xiang, who is in charge of performing arts in the human world, returned home at 10:00 PM on the 26th, cooked noodles, and went upstairs to sleep. Unexpectedly, the fire in the stove was not extinguished, and at 2:15 AM, the fire spread directly to the upper floor through the handrail. Liu woke up in shock when he heard people shouting outside the door. There was no way to escape. He wrapped his seven-year-old son A'er in a quilt and threw him out of the front window. Liu and his wife both jumped out of the window. Fortunately, the police arrived and caught them without injury. However, the maid Zhu Ma, the maid Mei Zhen, and the adopted daughter Ai Feng, who were sleeping in the back building, were unable to escape and were burned to death. The two children were already charred bones, and half of the maid's body was burned, which was terrible. The fire burned until about 3:00 AM before it was extinguished by fire trucks from various fire brigades. A total of eight wall doors and sixteen building tails were burned. Most of the residents were actors, and none of their clothes were moved out. The loss was about 50,000 to 60,000 yuan.

Hunan Provincial Government Strictly Orders to Maintain Education Fees

A Letter to the Headquarters of the Fourth Route Army to Stop the Military from Intercepting and Taking Education Salt Attached

Order the Salt Transport Bureau to Allocate 93,000 yuan per Month for Education Expenses

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan Province's education funds were originally allocated 93,000 yuan per month from the salt tax surcharge. The provincial government made overall arrangements to order the Hunan Coast Salt Transport Bureau to allocate it monthly. Therefore, in this time of financial distress, education funds can still maintain the status quo. Recently, salt taxes in various places have been intercepted locally by the managers of various divisions, which has caused the salt to be attached to education and the future of education to be extremely dangerous. The provincial government, according to the request of Chen Runlin and other representatives of the education community, forwarded a letter to the headquarters, strictly ordering each division not to directly intercept and take the salt to be attached to education fees, and ordering the Salt Affairs Audit Office and the Hunan Coast Salt Transport Bureau to allocate 93,000 yuan of education fees per month to maintain education, etc. It has been sent to the Hunan Coast Salt Bureau and the Salt Affairs Audit Office for compliance, and a letter has been sent to the headquarters of the Fourth Route Army for investigation and handling. The letter said, "The sender is Chen Runlin and other representatives of the education community, who are presenting the case of 93,000 yuan attached to salt, which is shaking. Please quickly send a letter to the Ministry to stop the interception and take it, and strictly order the bureaus to allocate it monthly to show faith and maintain education. I believe that the 93,000 yuan education funds in Hunan Province, which are allocated monthly from the salt attachment item, are the lifeblood of each school. Since the financial support telegram occurred, Jun Zuo ordered the Hunan Coast Salt Transport Bureau to allocate it monthly, hoping to obtain security and勉可Maintain the status quo, but the facts are getting poorer day by day. If it is not strictly implemented, it will be impossible to solve it. I have presented it to Jun Zuo in detail. I hope that Jun Zuo will approve the examination of the salt attachment that has been legally independent for ten items. The Central Government and Jun Fu have clearly designated the education of Tianyun, which is related to survival, and can be misappropriated. Now the schools are about to run out of food and are in danger. The principals of each school have held a full meeting and resolved that (1) they will present a letter to the provincial government to forward it to the commander-in-chief to strictly order each division not to directly intercept the salt and attach it to education fees, and (2) they will present a letter to the provincial government to strictly order the audit office and the salt transport bureau to comply with the above orders and allocate them monthly. 93,000 yuan will be allocated no later than the 10th of the following month, etc. The records are in the file and should be prepared in writing to earnestly request Jun Zuo to be mindful of the education students, and allow the transfer of the letter to the commander-in-chief to strictly order each division not to directly intercept the salt and attach it, and quickly strictly order the audit office and the salt transport bureau to comply with an order and allocate 93,000 yuan per month. No later than the 10th of the following month, complying with this request is imminent, and the survival of the school is at stake. The words of disclosure are extremely urgent and await orders. According to this investigation, education is the foundation of the country, and funding is the lifeblood of education. Since 53,000 yuan of the salt tax surcharge has been determined, it cannot be used for other purposes, which will hinder the progress of education. According to the above, if it is true, it should be strictly restricted to maintain education. The attached instructions and training orders to the Audit Office and the Salt Transport Bureau shall comply with them. The corresponding letter shall be sent to your department for investigation and handling. This is to say Yunyun."

The Ministry of Education通令The Education Department of each province and city shall order the Student Volunteer Army of each school to intensify training, Yuan Yunyun.

According to a letter from the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee, with the approval of the Central Secretariat, the Nanjing Special City Executive Committee was submitted for submission. The Second District Executive Committee submitted that since the Japanese army invaded and occupied my Liaoning and Jilin for more than two months, and the troops have not been withdrawn, it can be seen that it is deliberately provoking and destroying world peace. All party, government, and military agencies in the country, in view of the increasing brutality of the Japanese, have organized a volunteer army, but they should intensify training to prepare for driving the Japanese army out of the country. The 14th plenary session of the full district party members passed a resolution to submit a request to the Central Committee to pass a resolution to the Central Committee to order the national volunteer army to intensify training and prepare to drive the Japanese army out of the country. When the meeting passed, the 理合It was recorded in the file and presented to the Jun Association for review and presentation to the Central Government for implementation. With the approval of this, in addition to replying in a letter, it is urgently ordered to comply with this order.

Local News

Yesterday's Inauguration of the Joint Association of University Faculty and Staff

Thirty Member Representatives Elected

Since Zheng Hongnian, Chu Minyi, and others initiated the organization of the Joint Association of University Faculty and Staff, preparations began immediately. Two preparatory meetings were convened over a period of two weeks. The association then held its inaugural meeting yesterday morning at 10:00 AM in the auditorium of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA. The meeting passed a brief charter and elected thirty member representatives on the spot. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM. Details are recorded below:

Meeting Circumstances: Around 200 faculty and staff members from various schools arrived at the meeting successively by 10:00 AM. First, the music team of Jinan University played to commence the meeting. After the music, the master of ceremonies, Ren Qishan, shouted to mourn the compatriots in the Northeast who suffered misfortune. The members of the hall stood up unanimously and remained silent for three minutes. Then, Chairman Chu Minyi delivered an opening speech, briefly stating that today's inaugural meeting of the Joint Association of University Faculty and Staff is of extreme necessity. Although there have been many organizations among universities in Shanghai in the past, a universal, large-scale, and permanent group is still lacking. The organization of this association is suitable to this kind of need, and also embodies the meaning of a labor union. Labor unions are organizations for laborers, but intellectuals should also have such organizations to help each other, connect feelings, and be comforted both materially and spiritually. Especially in the midst of national crisis, education is the cultivation of national power, and our faculty and staff should work together. Today, all of you are joining this association. Please discuss the organization of this association in detail so that it can be healthy and complete. Next, He Tingshu reported on the preparation process, and Kang Xuanyi explained that the charter adopted a flexible constitution. Then, the charter was discussed, and representatives were elected. By this time, it was past noon. The entire body took a photograph and then took a temporary break. The ballots were counted in the afternoon until 6:00 PM, when the elected representatives were tallied. Zhang Shouyong and Hu Shuhua reported the election results and then adjourned the meeting. It was planned that the remaining recreational performances would be held later due to time constraints. It is heard that a grand recreational event will be held after the executive and supervisory committees are elected in the future.

Elected Representatives: A total of thirty member representatives were elected, listed below: Chu Minyi 105 votes, Wang Jingqi 91 votes, Zheng Hongnian 89 votes, Hu Shuhua 87 votes, Kang Xuanyi 79 votes, Li Yingbiao 70 votes, Li Zhaohuan 69 votes, Zhang Shouyong 68 votes, Lin Tongshi 56 votes, Li Denghui 53 votes, Lin Zhongke 51 votes, Fan Shouzhi 43 votes, Jiang Zhensan 43 votes, Chen Qifu 43 votes, Tang Ying 41 votes, He Tingshu 38 votes, Ren Qishan 38 votes, Ding Yao 38 votes, Sun Boqian 38 votes, Jing Yuanruo 37 votes, Yuan Shuibo 37 votes, Chen Qun 35 votes, Yan Fuqing 34 votes, Zhang Wenfu 32 votes, Yang Yufen 31 votes, Han Yanmen 31 votes, Hu Yaomei 29 votes, Chen Zhuzun 29 votes, Huang Xianzhang 28 votes, Deng Zhongying 37 votes. The above are the member representatives. The school representatives will be completely produced before January 5th. After the school representatives are produced, the association plans to hold a plenary meeting of all representatives at 3:00 PM on January 10th at the YMCA to elect the executive and supervisory committees.

Declaration of the General Assembly: Humans are social animals and cannot live in isolation. Therefore, "things gather by category, and people group by kind," and "similar sounds respond to each other, and similar spirits seek each other." Throughout history, regardless of China or foreign countries, ancient or modern times, human beings who are committed to the same cause constantly form a special organization due to the same living environment and the occurrence of spiritual communication. We, who dedicate ourselves to higher education, certainly cannot be excluded from the "universally applicable" public rules of humanity. There are numerous schools in this city, and talent is abundant, but the association is loose, like scattered sand. Past academic organizations were either limited to local areas or occurred temporarily, and were insufficient to meet universal needs or complete permanent missions. We deeply feel that this is a shortcoming and always think of ways to remedy it. This association has gathered the faculty and staff of various schools to initiate the association. All schools in the urban area, from principals to employees, are included regardless of academic faction, to gather the great achievements of thought and temper all parties in one furnace to address common problems, improve their own lives, exchange books, instruments, and equipment to make up for deficiencies, study advanced academics, discuss administrative courses, observe each other and be good, and follow the good. We will also proceed to statistically analyze talent, coordinate and cooperate, and strive to match supply and demand, allow people to use their talents to the fullest, and each get what they deserve. Other matters, such as establishing academic clubs to harmonize the lives of educators, creating educational banks to circulate academic finance, supporting educational progress, promoting Chinese culture, and restoring self-confidence, are all things that the association has planned day and night, constantly contemplating, researching, and thinking deeply, and striving to realize them. This association does not sing high-sounding tunes, make empty promises, or seek immediate results. We will take a roundabout route, be pragmatic, proceed gradually, and persevere. The great cause of culture is not the responsibility of others. All my colleagues, come!

Charter Passed: (1) Name: This association is named the Shanghai Joint Association of University Faculty and Staff. (2) Purpose: The purpose of this association is to connect feelings, study academics, promote culture, increase the interests of members, and cultivate national strength. (3) Membership: Anyone who is a faculty or staff member of a college or university in Shanghai can be a member of this association. (4) Meetings: The meetings of this association are divided into the following types: general meeting of members, meeting of representatives, executive committee meeting, supervisory committee meeting, and various other committee meetings. (A) The general meeting of members is held at least twice per academic year. If necessary, a special meeting may be convened upon the proposal of more than two-fifths of all members, or by the resolution of the executive committee or the meeting of representatives. (B) The meeting of representatives is held at least once a month. If necessary, a special meeting may also be convened upon the proposal of five representatives. (C) The executive committee meets once a week. (D) The supervisory committee is convened when necessary. (E) Various other meetings are determined by each committee. (5) The meeting of representatives is organized by member representatives and faculty and staff representatives from various schools. (A) Thirty member representatives are elected by the general assembly for a term of half a year and may be re-elected. (B) Each school elects faculty and staff representatives: two from each university and one from each independent college or vocational school. The term of office is one year and may be re-elected. (6) The association's executive committee has fifteen members and the supervisory committee has five members, elected by the meeting of representatives for a term of one year. (7) The executive committee may establish various specialized committees at any time and hire members to organize them. (8) The executive committee mutually elects five standing committee members to handle daily affairs. (9) The executive committee and the meeting of representatives each have two general affairs officers to manage affairs separately. (10) Membership fees are collected from each school and each member upon joining: 20 to 50 yuan per school and 1 yuan per member. Regular expenses are 20 to 50 yuan per month per school and 2 yuan per member per semester. Special donations are decided by the meeting of representatives and collected by the executive committee. (11) The association's office is located in Shanghai. (12) A quorum for various meetings of the association is more than one-half of the total number of people. (13) Matters not covered in this charter may be revised by the meeting of representatives.

Explanation of Entertainment: It is inappropriate for the student union of various universities to use music to celebrate the establishment of the association during the national crisis and should be warned. Yesterday, Mr. Kang of the association said to reporters that patriotism and entertainment do not conflict. In economics, there is the so-called "consumptive production," which means that production can be increased after consumption and entertainment. Music is not just for enjoyment. Songs of grief, anger, and heroism can inspire ambition, and sounds of sadness and lamentation can release sorrow. Therefore, golden horns and war drums are used to assist in battle, and stringed and bamboo instruments are used to express mourning. This cannot be discussed with a superficial view. Our patriotism can be expressed through art, and the power of art can promote our patriotic spirit. The two complement each other and are not contradictory. (Daily News)

Finance Last Week's Gold Market Stable, Rose by Thirteen Taels

Fluctuations of Thirty-Four Taels in the Market on the Fourth Day. The trend of bid gold was stable and firm last week, and the volatility was still not small, with daily fluctuations of twenty taels. However, due to the Christmas holiday, there were only four market days. The lowest morning opening at the beginning of the week was only 656.5 taels. On Tuesday, it once rushed to 690 taels and five mace, and then fell back, retreating 80 taels. The entire week had a review of 34 taels. In total, it rose by 13 taels and two mace. The overseas silver market and the Shanghai British and American exchange rates have slightly fallen, such as the British exchange rate shrinking by two gears and the American exchange rate leveling off. This is because the British and American exchange rates rose first and then fell, and then rose sharply. The internal situation of the bank seemed to be tense. The gold gang had some collusion to resist the previous short positions. Most of them were arbitrage transactions, and the arbitrage price gradually narrowed to only about thirty taels. As for the settlement price, it was pressed down by forty to fifty taels. All forward transactions that had not been completed were raised to nearly thirty taels due to pressure from the multi-party. However, on Thursday, Da Fengheng and other spot dealers dropped 11 taels from the spot house. In general, the chips were limited, and the spot was also scarce. As for burning red, it added fifteen or sixteen taels. Since the telegraphic exchange rate of Datiao Bank on the 24th slightly grew by zero six two five, there was no market on the 25th and 26th due to Christmas. The details of these four days are extracted below.

Because the US dollar was squeezed and the exchange rate was large, it grew by 375, and the domestic market was also very good.
